<text>I almost wish I had never eaten here because now that I have, I will be craving this every day.

I am a HUGE fan of Pho.  It's my favorite comfort food when I'm sick, my go-to when it's raining outside, or even when I'm just having a bad day.  I've eaten Pho in cities around the world and have had an assortment of tastes and accouterments. I will say that this vegetarian Pho, specifically the broth, is hands-down the best I've ever eaten.  I wish I could give it more stars.

Earthy and rich without being fatty, a great balance of flavors with just a hint of spice and acid.  Draw me a bath of this broth!

The toppings were interesting to me.  It was the first time I've been given cooked veggies and I was very surprised to find green beans.  I'm used to basil and sometimes chopped peanuts, but there were neither.  There was plenty of cilantro (no thanks!) and bean sprouts, plus some hot sauce (yes please!) and plum sauce (yum!).  The noodles were not gummy, which is AMAZING for take-away.  They were a joy to eat.

I got take-away and only the veggie Pho so I can attest to nothing else, but it is amazing!< /text><Rate>5<//Rate><Time>1554355332957<//Time><userid>106641706362298697859</userid>< Name>

I've been eyeing Proverbs 31 for some time now. I was attending my birthday bash on Saturday and thought I'd finally give them a try.¬† I scheduled a makeup appointment on Wednesday for Saturday at 3:00. Thursday I received a Text conforming my appointment and asking what I wanted as far as makeup and if I had any pictures of what I wanted. I informed Gabriel that I wanted something natural, neutral colors, nothing glittery or shimmery. Just a very simple look that accentuates my natural features. He said okay,¬† no problem. Friday afternoon I received a Text asking if I could come in Saturday either at 1:00 or 4:30 because there was a mix up with the artist who was going to be doing my makeup. I denied the alternative options and was told to keep the 3:00 slot and was also asked to bring my own foundation. I was somewhat baffled at the fact that I was asked to bring my foundation so I asked if the foundation was included in the makeup application. I was told that it was but in the event that I had sensitive skin,¬† I should proceed that route. I told Gabriel that I was not sensitive and I'd be there at 3:00 tomorrow. I thought this was odd and honestly I didn't like the encounter I had just had and wanted to cancel. However,¬† I knew that it was very unlikely that I'd get a last minute appointment somewhere else. So I gave them the benefit of the doubt, ignored the red flags and I showed up. This place specializes in eye lash application,¬† so there are beds everywhere. I shouldn't have ignored that.¬† So I was taken to a small corner desk where there were about 2 makeup bags. I was apprehensive about the whole ordeal but decided to stay. I sat on the desk chair, I repeated to her that I wanted something very natural looking,¬† neutral colors nothing too harsh. She said okay and off we went with the makeup application.¬† The makeup artist just went straight for it, she started shaping my eyebrows and¬† I could feel how she wasn't following my request.¬† Mind you,¬† at no point was I facing a mirror. So she finishes the eyes, applies the makeup, concealer, sprays my face then it's time for the mascara. She asked me to apply my own mascara and¬† that's when I got up and looked in the mirror. I was horrified and disappointed.¬† The brows looked like two caterpillars, the makeup was super heavy, the contour looked like tiger stripes and you could totally see the concealer packed underneath my eyes. Nothing was blended! They had initially told me that application took 45 min and we were approaching an hour.¬† I told her she needed to fix the brows because they were too much.¬† She was unsuccessful and at that point I knew I had to get out of there because I knew I wasn't going to get the result I wanted. I paid and ran to my car. Flustered by my time constraint, I knew there was no way I could go to my event looking like a cabaret girl. I called Sephora at Victoria gardens and explained to them that I had a makeup emergency and needed them to fix it. At this point I was IN TEARS! The thought of showing up to my party looking like a clown made me feel so so embarrassed.¬† So they managed to squeeze me in and much to their disdain and unbelief at the fact that my neck and face were two different colors,¬† they immediately asked, "who did this?!?" They were in disbelief that anyone would let me walk out of a makeup studio looking like that.¬† 45 min later, I walked out of Sephora looking like what I should have looked like in the first place-- amazing. NEVER again will I make this mistake. You don't see a lawyer for catering needs or go to a bakery for suit alterations.¬† If you want makeup done right,¬† go see someone who knows their craft,¬† not someone who focuses on lashes and does makeup on the side from their garage.
